Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on November 26, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











The Japanese Legacy community has always been supportive of local events and this is evidenced by the whooping 26 Grand Prix Trials which took place yesterday. If you think that's a lot of decklists, it's only the tip of the iceberg because what you see today is simply an inkling of Grand Prix Chiba's metagame this weekend!







#### Aaron De Silva's Death and Taxes


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)





[Decklist](#none)
[Stats](#none)
[Sample Hand](#none)
